./CHANGELOG.md:6211:In versions before Talos 1.9, there was a discrepancy between the way Talos itself and CRI plugin resolves registry mirrors:
./CHANGELOG.md:6212:Talos will never fall back to the default registry if endpoints are configured, while CRI plugin will.
./CHANGELOG.md:6214:> Note: Talos Linux pulls images for the `installer`, `kubelet`, `etcd`, while all workload images are pulled by the CRI plugin.
./CHANGELOG.md:6217:configuration option `.skipFallback` can be used to disable this behavior both for Talos and CRI plugin.

./CHANGELOG.md:8127:* **github.com/siderolabs/go-kubernetes**               v0.2.12 -> v0.2.13
./CHANGELOG.md:8165:Talos Linux now supports configuring Kubernetes node annotations via machine configuration (`.machine.nodeAnnotations`) in a way similar to node labels.
./CHANGELOG.md:8206:### Extensions in Kubernetes Nodes
./CHANGELOG.md:8208:Talos Linux now publishes list of installed extensions as Kubernetes node labels/annotations.
./CHANGELOG.md:8220:Usage of the host DNS resolver as upstream for Kubernetes CoreDNS pods is now enabled by default. You can disable it
./CHANGELOG.md:8228:      forwardKubeDNSToHost: false
./CHANGELOG.md:8234:For those upgrading from Talos 1.7 with `forwardKubeDNSToHost` enabled, the old Kubernetes service
./CHANGELOG.md:8235:can be cleaned up with `kubectl delete -n kube-system service host-dns`.
./CHANGELOG.md:8252:### Slim Kubelet Image
./CHANGELOG.md:8254:Kubelet container image includes various utilities that kubelet might use to perform various tasks.
./CHANGELOG.md:8256:Starting with Kubernetes 1.31.0, `kubelet` image now includes less utilities, as the in-tree CSI plugins were
./CHANGELOG.md:8257:removed in Kubernetes 1.31.0. This reduces `kubelet` image size and potential attack surface.
./CHANGELOG.md:8259: For Kubernetes < 1.31.0, there will be two images built:
./CHANGELOG.md:8264:For Kubernetes >= 1.31.0, there will be same two images built, but the
./CHANGELOG.md:8273:Talos Linux on config generation now adds a label `node.kubernetes.io/exclude-from-external-load-balancers` by default for the control plane nodes.
./CHANGELOG.md:8301:### kube-proxy
./CHANGELOG.md:8303:Talos Linux configures kube-proxy >= v1.31.0 to use 'nftables' backend by default.
./CHANGELOG.md:8323:Kubernetes: 1.31.0

./CHANGELOG.md:10967:### Kubelet Credential Provider Configuration
./CHANGELOG.md:10969:Talos now supports specifying the kubelet credential provider configuration in the Talos configuration file.
./CHANGELOG.md:10970:It can be set under `machine.kubelet.credentialProviderConfig` and kubelet will be automatically configured to with the correct flags.
./CHANGELOG.md:10971:The credential binaries are expected to be present under `/usr/local/lib/kubelet/credentialproviders`.
./CHANGELOG.md:10988:### Kube-Scheduler Configuration
./CHANGELOG.md:10990:Talos now supports specifying the kube-scheduler configuration in the Talos configuration file.
./CHANGELOG.md:10991:It can be set under `cluster.scheduler.config` and kube-scheduler will be automatically configured to with the correct flags.
./CHANGELOG.md:10994:### KubePrism
./CHANGELOG.md:10996:[KubePrism](https://www.talos.dev/v1.6/kubernetes-guides/configuration/kubeprism/) is enabled by default on port 7445.

./CHANGELOG.md:12110:### KubePrism - Kubernetes API Server In-Cluster Load Balancer
./CHANGELOG.md:12112:Talos now supports configuring the KubePrism - Kubernetes API Server in-cluster load balancer with machine config
./CHANGELOG.md:12113:`features.kubePrism.port` and `features.kubePrism.enabled` fields.
./CHANGELOG.md:12115:If enabled, KubePrism binds to `localhost` and runs on the same port on every machine in the cluster.
./CHANGELOG.md:12116:The default value for KubePrism endpoint is https://localhost:7445.
./CHANGELOG.md:12118:The KubePrism is used by the `kubelet`, `kube-scheduler`, `kube-controller-manager`
./CHANGELOG.md:12119:and `kube-proxy` by default and can be passed to the CNIs like Cilium and Calico.
./CHANGELOG.md:12121:The KubePrism provides access to the Kubernetes API endpoint even if the external loadbalancer
./CHANGELOG.md:12134:kubelet feature gate `LocalStorageCapacityIsolationFSQuotaMonitoring` to use xfs quotas
./CHANGELOG.md:12157:A new set of commands was introduced to manage container images in the CRI:
./CHANGELOG.md:12160:* `talosctl image pull` allows to pre-pull an image into the CRI
./CHANGELOG.md:12164:* `cri` (default): images managed by the CRI (Kubernetes workloads)
./CHANGELOG.md:12165:* `system`: images managed by Talos (`etcd` and `kubelet`)
./CHANGELOG.md:12202:* etcd: 3.5.9
./CHANGELOG.md:12203:* Kubernetes: 1.28.0-beta.0
./CHANGELOG.md:12209:### `talosctl upgrade-k8s` Image Pre-pulling
./CHANGELOG.md:12211:The command `talosctl upgrade-k8s` now by default pre-pulls images for Kubernetes controlplane components
./CHANGELOG.md:12212:and kubelet. This provides an early check for missing images, and minimizes downtime during Kubernetes

./CHANGELOG.md:13421:### Kubernetes API Server In-Cluster Load Balancer
./CHANGELOG.md:13423:Talos now supports configuring the Kubernetes API Server in-cluster load balancer with machine config
./CHANGELOG.md:13429:The in-cluster loadbalancer endpoint is used by the `kubelet`, `kube-scheduler`, `kube-controller-manager`
./CHANGELOG.md:13430:and `kube-proxy` by default and can be passed to the CNIs like Cilium and Calico.
./CHANGELOG.md:13432:The in-cluster loadbalancer provides access to the Kubernetes API endpoint even if the external loadbalancer
./CHANGELOG.md:13463:kubelet feature gate `LocalStorageCapacityIsolationFSQuotaMonitoring` to use xfs quotas

./CHANGELOG.md:14232:### etcd Maintenance
./CHANGELOG.md:14234:Talos adds new APIs to make it easier to perform etcd maintenance operations.
./CHANGELOG.md:14236:These APIs are available via new `talosctl etcd` sub-commands:
./CHANGELOG.md:14238:* `talosctl etcd alarm list|disarm`
./CHANGELOG.md:14239:* `talosctl etcd defrag`
./CHANGELOG.md:14240:* `talosctl etcd status`

./CHANGELOG.md:14861:### etcd Maintenance
./CHANGELOG.md:14863:Talos adds new APIs to make it easier to perform etcd maintenance operations.
./CHANGELOG.md:14865:These APIs are available via new `talosctl etcd` sub-commands:
./CHANGELOG.md:14867:* `talosctl etcd alarm list|disarm`
./CHANGELOG.md:14868:* `talosctl etcd defrag`
./CHANGELOG.md:14869:* `talosctl etcd status`
./CHANGELOG.md:14871:See also [etcd maintenance guide](https://talos.dev/v1.4/advanced/etcd-maintenance/).
./CHANGELOG.md:14918:rebooting, shutting down a node, accessing packet capture, etcd alarm APIs, etcd backup, etc.

./CHANGELOG.md:16413:### kube-apiserver Audit Policy
./CHANGELOG.md:16415:Talos now supports setting custom audit policy for `kube-apiserver` in the machine configuration.
./CHANGELOG.md:16465:kubepods
./CHANGELOG.md:16484:### CRI Configuration Overrides
./CHANGELOG.md:16486:Talos no longer supports CRI config overrides placed in `/var/cri/conf.d` directory.
./CHANGELOG.md:16488:[New way](https://www.talos.dev/v1.3/talos-guides/configuration/containerd/) correctly handles merging of containerd/CRI plugin configuration.
./CHANGELOG.md:16491:### etcd Consistency Check
./CHANGELOG.md:16493:Talos enables [--experimental-compact-hash-check-enabled](https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/pull/14120) option by default to improve
./CHANGELOG.md:16494:etcd store consistency guarantees.
./CHANGELOG.md:16496:This options is only available with etcd >= v3.5.5, so Talos doesn't support version of etcd before v3.5.5.
./CHANGELOG.md:16499:### etcd Member ID
./CHANGELOG.md:16501:Talos now internally handles etcd member removal by member ID instead of member name (hostname).
./CHANGELOG.md:16502:This resolves the case when member name is not accurate or empty (eg: when etcd hasn't fully joined yet).
./CHANGELOG.md:16504:Command `talosctl etcd remove-member` now accepts member IDs instead of member names.
./CHANGELOG.md:16509:talosctl get etcdmember
./CHANGELOG.md:16518:It works well with CCM and Kubernetes node autoscaler.
./CHANGELOG.md:16537:### KubeSpan
./CHANGELOG.md:16539:KubeSpan MTU link size is now configurable via `network.kubespan.mtu` setting in the machine configuration.
./CHANGELOG.md:16553:Changes to the node labels will be applied immediately without `kubelet` restart.
./CHANGELOG.md:16592:The directory "/etc/kubernetes/manifests" is now deprecated.
./CHANGELOG.md:16594:To reenable support you may set `machine.kubelet.disableManifestsDirectory`.

./CHANGELOG.md:18193:### etcd Consistency Check
./CHANGELOG.md:18195:Talos enables [--experimental-compact-hash-check-enabled](https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/pull/14120) option by default to improve
./CHANGELOG.md:18196:etcd store consistency guarantees.
./CHANGELOG.md:18198:This options is only available with etcd >= v3.5.5, so Talos doesn't support version of etcd before v3.5.5.

./CHANGELOG.md:18600:* **k8s.io/kubelet**                                 v0.25.0 -> v0.26.0-alpha.1
./CHANGELOG.md:18615:### Talos API access from Kubernetes
./CHANGELOG.md:18617:Talos now supports access to its API from within Kubernetes. It can be configured in the machine config as below:
./CHANGELOG.md:18622:    kubernetesTalosAPIAccess:
./CHANGELOG.md:18626:      allowedKubernetesNamespaces:
./CHANGELOG.md:18627:        - kube-system
./CHANGELOG.md:18631:Creating custom resources of this type will provide credentials to access Talos API from within Kubernetes.
./CHANGELOG.md:18633:The new CLI subcommand `talosctl inject serviceaccount` can be used to configure Kubernetes manifests with Talos service accounts as below:
./CHANGELOG.md:18636:kubectl apply -f manifests-injected.yaml
./CHANGELOG.md:18639:See [documentation](https://www.talos.dev/v1.2/advanced/configuration/talos-api-access-from-k8s/) for more details.
./CHANGELOG.md:18644:It is now possible to generate a secrets bundle from a Kubernetes PKI directory (e.g. `/etc/kubernetes/pki`).
./CHANGELOG.md:18650:This facilitates migrating clusters (e.g. created using `kubeadm`) to Talos.
./CHANGELOG.md:18653:talosctl gen secrets --kubernetes-bootstrap-token znzio1.1ifu15frz7jd59pv --from-kubernetes-pki /etc/kubernetes/pki
./CHANGELOG.md:18658:### Kubernetes ControlPlane Components
./CHANGELOG.md:18660:Talos now run all Kubernetes Control Plane Components with the CRI default Seccomp Profile and other recommendations as described in
./CHANGELOG.md:18661:[KEP-2568](https://github.com/kubernetes/enhancements/tree/master/keps/sig-cluster-lifecycle/kubeadm/2568-kubeadm-non-root-control-plane).
./CHANGELOG.md:18664:### Kubelet Default Runtime Seccomp Profile
./CHANGELOG.md:18666:Talos now runs Kubelet with the CRI default Seccomp Profile enabled.
./CHANGELOG.md:18667:This can be disabled by setting `.machine.kubelet.defaultRuntimeSeccompProfileEnabled` to `false`.
./CHANGELOG.md:18672:### Kubernetes Control Plane labels and taints
./CHANGELOG.md:18674:Talos now defaults to `node-role.kubernetes.io/control-plane` label/taint.
./CHANGELOG.md:18675:On upgrades Talos now removes the `node-role.kubernetes.io/master` label/taint on control-plane nodes and replaces it with the `node-role.kubernetes.io/control-plane` label/taint.
./CHANGELOG.md:18679:### Kubernetes Discovery Backend
./CHANGELOG.md:18681:Kubernetes cluster discovery backend is now disabled by default for new clusters.
./CHANGELOG.md:18683:causes issues for KubeSpan enabled clusters when control plane endpoint is KubeSpan-routed.
./CHANGELOG.md:18685:For air-gapped installations when the Discovery Service is not enabled, Kubernetes Discovery Backend can be enabled by applying
./CHANGELOG.md:18692:      kubernetes:
./CHANGELOG.md:18697:### KubeSpan Kubernetes Network Advertisement
./CHANGELOG.md:18699:KubeSpan no longer by default advertises Kubernetes pod networks of the node over KubeSpan.
./CHANGELOG.md:18701:and node-to-node traffic will be handled by KubeSpan.
./CHANGELOG.md:18704:Old behavior can be restored by setting `.machine.kubespan.advertiseKubernetesNetworks = true` in the machine config.
./CHANGELOG.md:18714:### `k8s.gcr.io` mirror configuration
./CHANGELOG.md:18716:Talos now defaults to adding a registry mirror configuration in the machineconfig for `k8s.gcr.io` pointing to both `registry.k8s.io` and `k8s.gcr.io` unless overridden.
./CHANGELOG.md:18717:This is in line with the Kubernetes 1.25 release having the new `registry.k8s.io` registry endpoint.
./CHANGELOG.md:18726:      k8s.gcr.io:
./CHANGELOG.md:18728:          - https://registry.k8s.io
./CHANGELOG.md:18729:          - https://k8s.gcr.io
./CHANGELOG.md:18774:Talos now supports creating custom seccomp profiles on the host machine which in turn can be used by Kubernetes workloads.
./CHANGELOG.md:18789:The profiles are created on the host under `/var/lib/seccomp/profiles` and bind mounted at `/var/lib/kubelet/seccomp/profiles` so Kubelet can use it.
./CHANGELOG.md:18791:See [documentation](https://www.talos.dev/v1.2/kubernetes-guides/configuration/seccomp-profiles/) for more details.
./CHANGELOG.md:18834:* Kubernetes: v1.25.0-beta.0

./CHANGELOG.md:21207:### Pinned Kubernets Version
./CHANGELOG.md:21209:Command `talosctl gen config` now defaults to Kubernetes version pinning in the generate machine configuration.
./CHANGELOG.md:21210:Previously default was to omit explicit Kubernetes version, so Talos picked up the default version it was built against.
./CHANGELOG.md:21211:Old behavior can be achieved by specifying empty flag value: `--kubernetes-version=`.

./website/content/v1.13/reference/configuration/v1alpha1/config.md:1950:|`listenSubnets` |[]string |The `listenSubnets` field configures the networks for the etcd to listen for peer and client connections.<br><br>If `listenSubnets` is not set, but `advertisedSubnets` is set, `listenSubnets` defaults to<br>`advertisedSubnets`.<br><br>If neither `advertisedSubnets` nor `listenSubnets` is set, `listenSubnets` defaults to listen on all addresses.<br><br>IPs can be excluded from the list by using negative match with `!`, e.g `!10.0.0.0/8`.<br>Negative subnet matches should be specified last to filter out IPs picked by positive matches.<br>If not specified, advertised IP is selected as the first routable address of the node.  | |
